STRING Plain flaps are the simplest type of flap. It is simply a control surface that pivots down, producing some extra lift and bit of drag.====簡單襟翼是各類襟翼中最簡單的一種。它是一個能夠繞指點向下旋轉，並提供更多升力與阻力的操縱面。
STRING Slotted flaps are a more effective type of flap. A 'slot' (or gap) between the flap and the wing SPEEDS THE AIR UP AS IT PASSES OVER THE FLAP, producing more lift. The wing pitches down more, though.====開縫襟翼是種更加有效的襟翼類型。襟翼與機翼間的一條開縫使空氣經過襟翼時加速，從而產生更多的升力——盡管這會讓機翼的俯仰向下一些。
STRING Slotted Fowler flaps move BACK AND DOWN when deployed. A 'slot' along the flap SPEEDS THE AIR UP OVER THE TOP OF THE FLAP, and keeps it from stalling as well, producing lots of extra lift.====開縫富勒襟翼展開時向後向下移動。襟翼與機翼間的一條開縫使空氣經過襟翼時加速，同時避免機翼失速，能夠產生大量的額外升力。
STRING Slotted Double-Fowler flaps moves BACK AND DOWN when deployed. Multiple 'slots' along the flap SPEED THE AIR UP OVER THE TOP OF THE FLAP, and keep it from stalling as well, producing lots of extra lift.====開縫富勒襟翼展開時向後向下移動。襟翼與機翼間的多條開縫使空氣經過襟翼時加速，同時避免機翼失速，能夠產生大量的額外升力。
STRING Slotted Triple-Fowler flaps moves BACK AND DOWN when deployed. Multiple 'slots' along the flap SPEED THE AIR UP OVER THE TOP OF THE FLAP, and keep it from stalling as well, producing lots of extra lift.====開縫富勒襟翼展開時向後向下移動。襟翼與機翼間的多條開縫使空氣經過襟翼時加速，同時避免機翼失速，能夠產生大量的額外升力。

STRING In reality, aircraft controls have near-infinite resolution, high displacement-force, and the plane imparts G on you when you pull back. To help make up for the lack of these things in the sim, you can slide these sliders up a bit to add 「auto-control」 displacements to stabilize the plane. It isn』t realistic, but may make the plane feel more realistic.====實際上, 飛機的操控系統有近乎無窮的分辨率及很高的位移力, 當你拉升時, 飛機會向你傳遞G力。為了彌補飛行模擬中的這些不足, 你可以滑動增加 "自動控制" 的滑塊來穩定飛機。這在現實中不存在, 但可能使模擬飛行感覺更真實。

STRING Real pilots fly in a very specific way during takeoff & landing. In this tutorial, you’ll learn to take off, fly a rectangular circuit, and land back on the runway just like you would in the real world.====真正的飛行員在起飛和著陸期間以非常特定的方式飛行。 在本教程中，您將像在現實世界中一樣學習起飛、飛行矩形電路並重新降落在跑道上。

STRING Anisotropic Filtering====各向異性過濾
STRING Increasing this slider makes runways and flat surfaces sharper from low angles. This impacts your graphics card, so if you have a very powerful graphics card, you can set this up to 8x or higher.====增加此滑塊可使跑道和平面從低角度變得更清晰。 這會影響您的顯卡，因此如果您有一個非常強大的顯卡，您可以將其設置為 8 倍或更高。
STRING Use %1:driver name% for faster rendering====使用 %1:driver name% 更快的渲染
STRING The %1:driver name% is faster than the default OpenGL driver and may improve your framerate. Not all third party plugins are compatible with the %2:driver name%; if your installed third party add-ons do not render correctly, disable this option and restart X-Plane.==== %1:driver name% 比默認的 OpenGL 驅動程序更快，並且可能會提高您的幀速率。 並非所有第三方插件都與 %2:driver name%; 兼容。 如果您安裝的第三方插件無法正確渲染，請禁用此選項並重新啟動 X-Plane。

STRING Each external visual can either have its view locked to this machine’s (useful for linking together many computers to show the scenery), or its view can be independent of this machine (useful if you want to have one machine always display your instrument panel, for instance, even when your master machine is in an external view).====每個外部視覺都可以將其視圖鎖定到這台機器的視圖（用於將多台計算機連接在一起以顯示風景），或者它的視圖可以獨立於這台機器（如果您想讓一台機器始終顯示您的儀表板，這很有用，例如 例如，即使您的主機在外部視圖中）。
STRING Use this section to set another simulator on your local network to act as this machine’s master simulator, so that this machine will act as an extension of the master simulator’s displays.====使用此部分設置本地網絡上的另一個模擬器作為這台機器的主模擬器，這樣這台機器將作為主模擬器顯示器的擴展。
STRING You can configure this machine’s view relative to the master using the Graphics tab above.====您可以使用上面的圖形選項卡配置此機器相對於主機的視圖。
STRING If you want a suffix to always be added to the end of the aircraft folders we open on this computer, check this box and enter the suffix below. This is useful if you have two aircraft models, one with the pilot-side cockpit and the other with the copilot-side cockpit, with “Aircraft Folder\My Aircraft.acf” on the master computer, and “Aircraft Folder-copilot\My Aircraft.acf” on an external cockpit, for example. In that case, you would enter “-copilot” as the suffix (on the external cockpit computer only).====如果您希望始終將後綴添加到我們在這台計算機上打開的飛機文件夾的末尾，請選中此框並輸入下面的後綴。 如果您有兩個飛機模型，一個帶有飛行員側駕駛艙，另一個帶有副駕駛側駕駛艙，這很有用，主計算機上有“Aircraft Folder\My Aircraft.acf”，“Aircraft Folder-copilot\My 例如，外部駕駛艙上的 Aircraft.acf”。 在這種情況下，您將輸入“-copilot”作為後綴（僅在外部駕駛艙計算機上）。

STRING The controls should be centered, with the exception of any trim needed to hold level, un-accelerated flight. The autopilot may be on, since it will not have time to affect the test results.====操縱系統應居中，除了保持水平、非加速飛行所需的任何配平外。自動駕駛儀可能會開啟，由於它不會有時間影響測試結果。
STRING X-Plane will now instantly displace the nose exactly 1 degree, and look at the instantaneous acceleration back to trim of the craft, before the autopilot can respond.====X-Plane現在將立即移動機鼻正好1度，然後在自動駕駛儀作出反應之前，查看它的瞬時加速度以及恢複配平的過程。
STRING By looking at that acceleration, X-Plane will know the stability derivative. X-Plane will output its findings to the end of the 「Cycle Dump.txt」 file for you to see.====通過查看該加速度，X-Plane將會得知其穩定性導數。X-Plane會將其結果輸出到「Cycle Dump.txt」文件的結尾，以供您查閱。

STRING You extended the flaps above Vfe_kts.====你在高於最大襟翼伸出速度的速度放出了襟翼。
STRING The aircraft was carrying ice at time of impact.====飛機在墜毀前結冰。
STRING To prevent this in the future, stay out of the clouds and precip when temperatures are near freezing.====為了防止這種情況再次出現，當溫度接近冰點時避開雲層和降水。
STRING The aircraft was carrying carburetor ice at time of impact.====飛機的化油器在墜毀前結冰。
STRING To prevent this in the future, use carb heat when at low power in these weather conditions.====為了防止這種情況再次出現，在這種天氣條件下，在低功率時使用汽化器加熱。
STRING Use carb heat on carbureted engines when operating with engine RPM below the green arc.====在發動機轉速低於綠色弧線的情況下使用化油器式發動機的汽化器加熱。
STRING Failed to initialize UDP network input.====無法初始化UDP網絡輸入。
STRING This is almost certainly because you are already running another copy of X-Plane on the same computer.====這應該是因為您已經在同一台計算機上運行了X-Plane。
STRING Another possibility is that you turned off IPv6 support in your operating system. X-Plane requires at least link-local IPv6 connectivity.====另一種可能性是您在操作系統中關閉了IPv6支持。 X-Plane至少需要本地IPv6連接。
STRING Be sure that IPv6 support is on, and restart your computer to be sure that no other instance of X-Plane is running in the background.====確保IPv6支持已啟用，並重新啟動計算機以確保沒有其他X-Plane程序在後台運行。
STRING Failed to initialize UDP network output.====無法初始化UDP網絡輸出。
STRING Networking beacon initialization failed.====網絡信標初始化失敗。
STRING This indicates a problem with your local network.====這表示您的本地網絡出現問題。
STRING You will be able to use X-Plane normally, but X-Plane will be unable to automatically configure networking.====您將能夠正常使用X-Plane，但X-Plane將無法自動配置網絡。
STRING You might try restarting your computer to shut down any other programs that might be using the same port, preventing X-Plane from being able to use it.====您可能會需要重新啟動計算機以關閉可能使用相同端口的任何其他程序，以防X-Plane無法使用所需的端口。
STRING Could not initialize networking.====無法初始化網絡。
STRING This means that your operating system does not seem to have a working ethernet or wi-fi adapter.====您的操作系統似乎沒有工作的以太網或Wi-Fi適配器。
STRING This may be because you have intentionally disabled your network adapter, or you may need to manually install drivers for your network adapter.====這可能是因為您有意禁用網絡適配器，或是您需要手動安裝網絡適配器的驅動程序。
STRING You will not be able to use multiplayer or other network features until this is fixed.====直到問題被修複，您將不能使用多人模式或其他需要網絡的功能

STRING You are going after a forest fire with no water to drop on it.====你要在沒有水可用的情況下趕往一場森林火災的現場。
STRING You might consider opening the Bombardier Seaplane, which packs a lot of water to dump on the fire.====你可以考慮駕駛龐巴迪水上飛機，它飛機可以攜帶很多的滅火用水。
STRING Skim the surface of any water to pick up a load of water. Then, fly your approach to the fire and jettison the water load over the fire to put part of the fire out.====從水面上滑過來給飛機裝水。然後，飛近火場並放水來撲滅一部分火。
STRING What you are planning to put on the fire will not be enough to extinguish it.====你打算澆在火上的水不足以撲滅它。
STRING No forest fires in the area.====這個區域沒有森林火災。
STRING Try moving to a mountainous area, where fires are more likely.====試著飛到山區去，那裏更容易發生火災。
STRING Also be sure there is no rain and the temperature is above 15° Celsius.====請確認那裏沒有下雨並且溫度高於15度。
STRING You can set this in the Customize Weather window.====您可以在自定義天氣窗口來設置這些情況。
STRING This will start you off 5,340 miles downrange at 450,000 feet and 15,400 mph.====這將您置於距離著陸場5430哩，450,000英尺的高空中；您的速度是15,400英裏每小時。
STRING The re-entry takes a long time and is an extreme challenge.====再入需要很長時間，同時是一項困難的挑戰。
STRING Watch the right EFIS to fly the vertical part of the re-entry, and the middle EFIS for the horizontal guidance to Edwards AFB.====觀察你右側的EFIS來執行再入的垂直部分；中間的EFIS會指引你到愛德華茲空軍基地。
STRING If you have too much speed, pull up to a higher pitch for more drag, and do steep S-turns to descend.====如果你速度太大，把機頭抬高來增加阻力，同時做深S彎來下降高度。
STRING This will be the final 12 minute glide to Edwards AFB, and is a moderate challenge.====這是滑翔到愛德華茲空軍基地的最後12分鍾，是難度適中的挑戰。
STRING This will start you off 40 miles downrange at 83,000 feet, Mach 2.5.====這將您置於距離著陸場40裏，83,000英尺的高空中；您的速度是2.5馬赫。
STRING Edwards AFB will be the small circle on your moving map. The large circle is the final turn.====愛德華茲空軍基地在你的移動地圖上是一個小圓圈。大的圓圈是你的最終轉彎航線
STRING Fly over and past Edwards at 60,000 feet, then do a left 230 degree turn to bring it back to Edwards for a landing on 22.====以60,000英尺的高度飛越愛德華茲基地，然後左轉航向230來返回愛德華茲基地以在22跑道著陸。
STRING Near the end, your descent path should be about 20 degrees down, 300 knots indicated.====快要結束時你的下滑角應該是向下20度，指示空速300節。
STRING This will start you off on an 8 mile final at 18,000 feet, 300 knots indicated.====這將您置於距離著陸場8裏的五邊進近，高度18,000英尺，速度300節。
STRING Edwards AFB will be right in front of you, and the glidelsope lighting will be a few miles short of Edwards.====愛德華茲空軍基地在正前方；下滑道指示燈在愛德華茲基地的幾英裏外。
STRING Fly the approach at 300 knots, aiming for the lights a few miles short of Edwards, then level out your descent over the lights.====進近速度為300節，飛向愛德華茲基地幾英裏外的引進燈，在燈的上方拉平
STRING After this 'Pre-Flare', where you level your descent, get the gear down and touch down smoothly.====在這個「預拉平」的位置拉平下降，放下起落架然後做一個平穩的著陸。
STRING You will now be towed aloft by another plane.====你將會被另一架飛機拖到高處。
STRING Your goal is to hold formation behind the towplane, not pulling to either side.====你的目標就是在牽引機後面保持隊形，不要去其他地方。
STRING Drop the cable when you are ready to glide on your own.====當你准備好自己滑翔時就放開拖繩
STRING You may try this with any glider, including ones you design in Plane Maker.====你可以用任何滑翔機嘗試它——包括您自己在Plane Maker中的設計。
STRING You will now try to fly the refueling probe of your airplane to within a few feet of the probe on the refueler craft and hold it there.====你現在要嘗試用你的受油管對准幾英尺以外的加油機的加油管並保持住。
STRING You will receive fuel as you do this.====這樣做時你的飛機會被加油。
STRING You should probably try this in a fighter like the F-4 Phantom.====你最好用像F-4鬼怪一類的戰斗機來嘗試這個任務。
STRING You can try this in any plane with a refueling probe, including ones you design in Plane Maker.====你可以用任何有受油管的飛機來嘗試這個任務，包括您自己在Plane Maker中的設計。
STRING You will now be dropped from the wing of another airplane. (The B-52 in cruise configuration is the default.)====你將會由其他飛機機翼下投放。（默認載機為巡航狀態的B-52）
STRING If you are in the X-15, you can then proceed to fly at full throttle to the edge of space.====若您在X-15中，您可以繼續將其在最大節流閥狀態下駕駛直至宇宙的邊緣。
STRING This will burn the paint off the aircraft in only one flight.====這將使得塗料在僅僅一次飛行後燒盡。
STRING X-15's sometimes blew up or crashed. Presumably your life insurance is up to date.====X-15飛機不時爆炸或墜毀。我們估計，您的人身保險還有效。

STRING X-Plane uses an aerodynamic model called 「blade element theory.」 X-Plane actually models the virtual airflow over the airfoil surfaces of the simulated aircraft. Most simulators use a table lookup scheme which can only approximate a correct flight model.====X-Plane使用的氣動模型叫做「槳葉剖面理論」。X-Plane實際上用虛擬的氣流吹過模擬模型的表面來模擬氣動情況。大多數的模擬軟件使用已有的數據表格，這只能模擬出近似的飛行模型。

STRING It』s sometimes desirable to start your aircraft on a 3 mile (VFR) or 10 mile (IFR) final to any runway. Use the drop down to select the appropriate distance for the runway you would like at your selected field.====有時候你需要飛機距離跑道3海裏（目視飛行規則）或者是10海裏（儀表飛行規則），你可以通過飛行設置>自定義並將狀態切換到跑道，通過下拉菜單來選擇到達你想要的跑道的適當距離
STRING MSL is an aviation term used to denote 「altitude above mean sea level.」 The altimeters in aircraft measure altitude above mean sea level and not above ground level. The term AGL means 「above ground level」 and radio altimeters are used to report altitudes in AGL.====MSL是航空界中用於表達「標准海平面高度」的縮寫，飛機中的高度計中現實的是海平面高度而不是地平面高度。而縮寫AGL的意思是「地面高度」，並且無線電高度表是以AGL來顯示高度的
STRING The Airspeed Indicator in the aircraft will read 「Indicated Airspeed,」 or IAS. The error in this value will increase the higher you fly (as the density of the surrounding air decreases).====飛機中的空速指示器被讀作「指示空速」，或者稱為"IAS"。這個值的誤差將會隨著你飛行高度的升高（空氣密度的減小）而增加
STRING It』s easier than ever to run X-Plane on multiple monitors. Go to Settings > Graphics > Monitor Configuration and configure each of the monitor boxes how you want it. Move the pop up windows for ATC, GPS, or maps to the other monitors if you like!====在X-Plane上即使用多個顯示器運行也十分容易。只需要前往設置>顯示>顯示器設置並按照你的需求設置每個顯示器的顯示內容即可。

STRING Understanding the aerodynamic forces on an airplane will give you a better concept of how the aircraft flies. The four basic forces are weight, lift, thrust, and drag. Understanding the interaction of these forces will help you become a better pilot.====理解空氣動力學可以給你一個更好的概念來理解飛機是如何飛行的。四大基本力是重量，升力，推力和阻力。了解這些力的關系可以幫助你成為一名更好的飛行員。
STRING POH stands for 「Pilot Operating Handbook」 and contains aircraft operational information. Most POH can be obtained on the internet by searching for your aircraft and the phrase 「POH.」====POH的意思是「飛行員操作手冊」，包含了飛機的操作信息。大多數的POH可以在網上通過搜索你想要的機型加上"POH"關鍵字查找到。

STRING 「Controlled airspace」 is airspace of defined dimensions. Pilots should become familiar with the types of controlled airspace and the restrictions for flying within it. X-Plane, along with the appropriate charts and airspace documentation, is the perfect way to practice staying legal.====「控制空域」是限制飛入的地區，飛行員應該熟記各種類型的控制區域並在飛入時遵守這些規定。X-Plane同樣參考了航圖和空域文件，是訓練合法飛越的完美途徑

STRING One of the best training books for pilots is over a half-century old: 「Stick and Rudder」 by Wolfgang Langewiesche.====最佳的飛行員訓練書籍之一已經有半個世紀老了：Wolfgang Langewiesche所著的"Stick and Rudder"（注：全名為Stick and Rudder: An Explanation of the Art of Flying;在某東可以買到）
STRING Take on a new challenge in X-Plane and learn to fly a tail-dragger. Open Flight Configuration and select the Stinson L5, or try the Taildragger Takeoff Tutorial. Better practice up on your stick and rudder skills for this challenge.====在X-Plane中發掘全新的挑戰：試著飛一架後三點起落架布局的飛機；前往飛行設置頁面並選擇史丁森L5，或者試試後三點式起落架飛機起飛教程。這個挑戰會很好的鍛煉你的「杆子和尾舵」的技巧
STRING Simulate an engine failure right after takeoff. Can you make the airport or do you land straight ahead? Try it with different wind directions and wind velocities. Now try changing the fuel and passenger loading. Can you survive this emergency under instrument conditions?====模擬起飛後引擎失效的情況，你是會返回機場還是徑直降落？試著用不同的風向和風速來模擬特情；接下來試著用不同的燃油量和乘客配載，你能在這樣的條件下存活下來麼？
STRING Adding takeoff power to a single-engine aircraft in X-Plane will cause the plane to veer to the left. This effect also occurs in real aircraft and is caused by engine torque and by the propeller wash over the wings. Compensate for this effect by applying right rudder during takeoff and climb.====在X-Plane中對單發飛機設置起飛推力會使飛機左偏，這種情況在真機上也會出現，是由發動機力矩和螺旋槳吹過機翼的氣流造成的。補償這種效果需要在起飛和爬升期間向右蹬舵。

STRING Want a different flying experience for a change? Try the glider tow. Go to Flight Configuration and pick a glider. Hit the Customize button and pick Tow Plane. You will be towed aloft and you will choose when to release the tow line.====想要來點不一樣的挑戰經曆？試試滑翔機拖機吧。前往飛行設置並選擇一架滑翔機。按下自定義按鈕選擇一架滑翔機拖機。你會被拖到高空然後自行判定什麼時候斷開拖繩。

STRING Groundspeed is the actual speed that an aircraft travels over the ground. It is the combination of the aircraft』s airspeed and the wind's speed relative to the aircraft's direction.====地速是反應飛行器相對地面速度的數值。它由飛機空速和飛機朝向所決定

STRING Do you notice a yawing movement as you enter a turn? This is called 「adverse yaw」 and is caused by the lifting wing. Counter this tendency by applying rudder in the direction of the turn.====你注意到當你開始轉彎的時候有輕微的偏航麼？這是由抬升一側機翼造成的「不利偏航」，抵消這個動作只需反向蹬舵。
STRING Be a top gun and 「call the ball.」 Try landing your fighter jet on the deck of an aircraft carrier. Go to Flight Configuration > Location > Customize > Special Starts, then select the Carrier Approach line. Make sure you』re flying a fighter such as the F-4 Phantom, or perhaps a jet that you designed with Plane Maker.====像電影《壯志淩雲》中一樣"Call the Ball"。試試在航母上降落一架戰斗機。前往飛行設置>地點>自定義>特殊情況，然後選擇航母進近線。確保你飛的是像F-4鬼怪一樣的戰斗機，也可能是您用Plane Maker自己設計的噴氣機(注：當要在航母上降落的時候會有一支光束指引飛機以最優方式進近，以飛行員的視角來看這支光束會呈球形，當飛行員"Call the ball"的時候證明他目視到了光束並准備落地，這支光束也被叫做「上下視覺輔助」
STRING A flare in an airplane is not what you use when you have a flat tire. It is the simple maneuver performed moments before touchdown in which the nose is pitched up. This reduces the descent rate and causes the aircraft to touch down on the main wheels first.====飛機中的拉平不是只有在你輪胎漏氣時候來做。這只是一個你在接地之前抬高機鼻的簡單步驟。這回減小飛機的下降率並讓主起落架先接地
STRING When you get tired of flying, let X-Plane AI take control of your aircraft, views, or both. Select Flight > AI Flies Your Aircraft or AI Controls Your Views from the menu.====當你飛累了的時候，讓X-Plane的AI來接手飛機控制權，調整視角或同時進行。選擇菜單欄上的飛行>AI飛行飛機或者是AI控制視角
STRING If you』ve tried the glider tow and want something a little more exciting, try the winch. Go to Flight Configuration and pick a glider. Hit the Customize button and pick Glider Winch.====如果你已經試過了滑翔機拖機並還想找點新鮮刺激的事情來做，試試絞盤。前往飛行設置界面並選擇一架滑翔機，點擊自定義按鍵來裝上滑翔機絞盤。
STRING Did you know a nautical mile is a unit of distance equal to 1.15 statute miles, and one knot (a unit of speed) is defined as one nautical mile per hour?====你知道1海裏等於1.15英裏，1節（速度單位）等於1英裏每小時麼？
STRING Be a hit at the airshow flying your aerobatic plane and turn on the smoke. Hit the 『x』 key to toggle smoke, or pick a different key in Settings > Keyboard.====駕駛你的特技飛機在航展上拉著煙大顯身手。按下X鍵來放出煙霧，或者是在設置>鍵盤頁面設置一個不同的按鍵
STRING Running low on fuel? Try the mid-air refueling! Go to Flight Configuration > Location > Customize > Special Starts and pick Refuel-Boom or Refuel-Basket. Make sure you』re flying a fighter such as the F-4 Phantom, or perhaps a jet that you designed with Plane Maker.====飛著飛著要沒油了？試試空中加油！前往飛行設置>地點>自定義>特殊情況來選擇一個加油吊籃或者是加油管。確保你所飛行的是類似F-4鬼怪的戰斗機，或者是你自己在飛機制作器裏制作的噴氣機。
STRING A stall in an aircraft is a sudden loss of lift when the angle of attack is too high. This is initiated by the steep raising of an aircraft's nose, resulting in a loss of velocity and an abrupt drop. Correct this by immediately by lowering the nose and adding power.====飛行上的失速是在高攻角情況下突然失去升力的現象。一般始於機頭急劇上升，造成速度和高度急劇降低，通過壓低機鼻並增加推力的方式來改出。
STRING You can fly the X-15 rocket plane to the edge of space. Go to Flight Configuration > Location > Customize > Special Starts and pick Air Drop from B-52. Hit the space key to release, add power, and watch the sky turn from blue to black.====你可以飛行X-15火箭飛機前往大氣邊緣。前往飛行設置>地點>特殊情況並選擇從B-52上空投，按下空格鍵來釋放，增加推力，然後看著天空的顏色由藍變黑。
STRING Indicated airspeed (IAS) is the airspeed read directly from the airspeed indicator. It is the difference between total pressure and static pressure, and shows the dynamic pressure.====指示空速(IAS)是直接從空速計上上讀取的速度值。它是總壓和靜壓之間的值，指示了動壓。
STRING You can accurately simulate thermal activity in X-Plane. Go to Flight Configuration > Weather > Customize and adjust thermal coverage, tops, and climb rate.====你可以在X-Plane中設置熱活動。前往飛行設置>天氣>自定義來設置熱覆蓋，頂峰和爬升率
STRING When flying an instrument approach you should make your land/miss decision at the decision height. Decision height for approaches at various airports can be found on printed approach charts, as well as online. Not having visual contact with the airport at decision height will lead to a missed approach.====當執行儀表進近的時候你需要在決斷高度決斷著陸/複飛。各個機場的決斷高度可以在印好進近航圖上找到，在線亦可。如果在決斷高度沒有目視到機場就要複飛
STRING Want to try the ultimate challenge? Try landing the Space Shuttle. Go to Flight Configuration > Location > Customize. Click the Special Starts button and pick one of the 4 shuttle entry points. You can do a full re-entry from space all the way down to starting the flight on the final approach.====想要挑戰極限？試試降落航天飛機。前往飛行設置>地點>自定義。點擊特殊情況按鍵並選擇4個航天飛機再入點中的一個。你可以執飛一個完整的再入程序來做最終進近。
STRING Strap yourself in an X-Plane helicopter and land on a floating oil platform. Go to Flight Configuration > Location > Customize. Click the Special Starts button and pick a small or large oil rig approach.====駕駛一架X-Plane的直升機上然後降落在浮動燃油平台上。前往飛行設置>地點>自定義，點擊特殊開始按鍵來選擇一個小或大的燃油鑽井平台進近。
STRING Automatic Terminal Information Services, or ATIS, broadcast airport information on a continuous basis. Always listen to the ATIS transmission before contacting air traffic control at a controlled airport. ATIS frequencies for towered airports can be found on aeronautical maps and airport documentation. Similar information is broadcast at some non-towered airfields from automatic weather stations and is called AWOS.====自動航站情報服務（Automatic Terminal Information Services)或簡稱ATIS，是一個會持續播報機場基礎信息的廣播。記得每次聯系機場管制員之前先聽一下ATIS，ATIS的頻率會在杭圖上或者是機場文件上找到。相似的信息也會在一些無塔機場通過自動天氣基站廣播，名字叫做AWOS（Automatic Weather Observing System自動天氣觀測系統）。
STRING You can build your own 3-D airports and submit them for inclusion in future updates to X-Plane 11. Visit the X-Plane Scenery Gateway (gateway.x-plane.com) for more information.====你可以建造你自己的3-D機場並在未來的X-Plane11升級更新中發布他們。請訪問X-Plane Scenery Gateway (gateway.x-plane.com) 以了解更多信息。
STRING You can ask questions and help others on the X-Plane Question & Answer site. Go to questions.x-plane.com to join the community.====你可以在X-Plane的問答界面提出問題或者幫助其他人解決他們的問題。前往questions.x-plane.com來加入討論。

STRING Real pilots fly in a very specific way during takeoff & landing. In this tutorial, you』ll learn to take off, fly a rectangular circuit, and land back on the runway just like you would in the real world.====真正的飛行員在起降過程中會有特定的飛行方式，在這個教程中，你將會學習如何起飛，飛一個矩形航跡（本場起落航線），然後回到你起飛的跑道，正如在現實世界中一樣。

STRING X-Plane Basics====X-Plane的基本技巧
STRING Welcome to X-Plane. Here, you』ll learn the basics of flying in X-Plane: controlling the plane, changing the view, & more.====歡迎來到X-Plane。在這裏你將會學習用X-Plane飛行的基本功：控制飛機，變更視角和更多的操作
STRING Helicopter Basics====直升機基礎
STRING Forget everything you know about flying... this is a whole new world. In this tutorial, you』ll learn the fundamentals of taking off and controlling a helicopter.====忘掉你所知道的有關飛行的一切.......這是個全新的世界。在本教程中，你將會學習起飛和控制一架直升機的基本技巧。
STRING We want to set down right on the "29" numbers painted on the runway.====我們想要在標有「29」數字的跑道上落下來。
STRING Whoa! We weren』t ready to land yet...====哇！我們還沒准備好落地呢.......
STRING Landing in the Cessna 172====降落一架塞斯納172
STRING Landing an airplane can be incredibly daunting. Take it one step at a time, though, and you can learn to pilot the Cessna 172 safely down to the ground in no time.====降落一架飛機會讓人心生畏懼。經過循序漸進地學習，你就會學到飛行員是如何安全地降落一架塞斯納172的。
STRING Out of bounds!====超出範圍了！
STRING Way to go!====走你！
STRING We』re too high to land safely. I』m going to call the landing off.====我們要想安全落地的話太高了。我要終止落地。
STRING We』re going too fast to land safely. I』m going to call the landing off.====我們要想安全落地的話速度太快了。我要終止落地。
STRING Flying an ILS Approach====飛一個ILS進近
STRING An airport』s Instrument Landing System is designed to provide guidance for both your course and descent during a landing. If you want to fly a landing the way real-world pilots do, this is it.====機場的儀表進近系統是為了向你提供降落的航向和垂直引導而設計。如果你想要以真實世界中的飛行員的方式來落地的話，這就是你要的。
STRING Runway 34R, you』re cleared to land.====跑道34右，許可落地。
STRING We』re off course! We were supposed to be maintaining heading 160, but we』re too far west.====我們偏離徑向線了！我們希望保持在航向160，但是我們偏西太多了。
STRING We』re off course! We were supposed to be maintaining heading 160, but we』re too far east.====我們偏離徑向線了！我們希望保持在航向160，但是我們偏東太多了。
STRING We』re too low... We were supposed to be maintaining 5,000 ft.====我們太低了......我們應該保持在5000英尺。
STRING Soon, ATC will contact us and have us turn perpendicular to the runway, entering the base phase of the approach. Until then, we just follow their last instruction: heading 160 at 5,000 ft.====不久之後，ATC就會聯系我們並且讓我們轉到垂直跑道的位置，進入四邊准備進近。到那時，我們只需要遵循他們最後的指令：維持五千英尺高度轉航向160。
STRING Turn left heading 070, descend and maintain 3,000 ft.====左轉航向070，下3000英尺。
STRING We』re too high... we were supposed to be maintaining 3,000 ft.====我們太高了......我們應該保持在3000英尺。
STRING We』re too low... we were supposed to be maintaining 3,000 ft.====我們太低了.......我們應該保持在3000英尺。
STRING We』re off course... we were supposed to be turning to heading 070 at 3,000 ft.====我們偏離徑向線了......我們本應保持070航向維持3000英尺高度。
STRING We』re off course... We were supposed to be turning to heading 070 at 3,000 ft.====我們偏離徑向線了......我們本應保持070航向維持3000英尺高度。
STRING We』re off course... We were supposed to be flying the ILS to runway 34R, but we』re too far west.====我們偏離徑向線了......我們本應飛34右的ILS，但是我們偏西太多了。
STRING We』re off course... We were supposed to be flying the ILS to runway 34R, but we』re too far east.====我們偏離徑向線了......我們本應飛34右的ILS，但是我們偏東太多了。
STRING We』re at the threshold of the runway... be sure to make visual contact with the runway as you set the plane down.====我們在跑道入口，確保你能目視到跑道上你准備接地的接地點。
STRING Landing an Airliner====降落一架民航客機
STRING Landing the hulking, lumbering 737 requires a lot more precision than a general aviation plane. If you』ve mastered landing in the Cessna 172, give it a try.====降落一架笨重的，隆隆作響的737需要比降落一架通航飛機更加精准的操作。如果你降落塞斯納172的技術爐火純青，來試試這個。
STRING Uh... we didn't make it to the runway...====額......咱們沒能飛到跑道
STRING You didn』t land on our target runway...====你沒有落到目標跑道上......
STRING You did it!====你做到了！
STRING Taildragger Takeoff====後三點式飛機起飛
STRING Flying a taildragger requires a very different technique than a 「tricycle」-gear plane like the Cessna 172. The most popular taildraggers are used for landing on rugged or unpaved runways, or even in fields.====飛一架後三點式起落架的飛機需要與像塞斯納172這種前三點布局的飛機完全不同的技巧。後三點式飛機通常用來在降落在崎嶇的或者是未鋪裝的跑道，甚至是野地裏。

STRING Split flaps lower the bottom surface of the wing, but the top surface of the wing remains stationary! This produces a high-drag 'wedge'. You get lots of lift, but tons of drag!====分裂式襟翼展開時降下機翼底面，但機翼的頂面保持靜止。這產生了一個高阻力的「楔形」。注意，這將使得你在獲得大量升力的同時產生大量阻力。
STRING A Krueger flap extends out of the LEADING EDGE of the wing to manage the airflow to delay the onset of a stall, allowing slower flight at higher angles of attack without stalling.====克魯格襟翼從機翼的前緣伸出，並整理氣流以降低失速的臨界速度，從而允許飛行器在更高的迎角下更慢地飛行而不會失速。
STRING A slat extends forwards out of the LEADING EDGE of the wing to manage the airflow and form a slot to allow hi-energy air to flow through it to delay the onset of a stall, allowing slower flight at higher angles of attack without stalling.====縫翼從機翼的前緣向前延伸，並整理氣流，形成一個槽，使高能空氣能夠流過，從而降低失速的臨界速度，並允許飛行器在更高的迎角下更慢地飛行而不會失速。
STRING corrugated with gaps-smooth with gaps-smooth with no gaps-high energy slots====波紋，有縫的-平滑，有縫的-平滑，無縫的-高能量槽縫

STRING At this point, when you look at your CDI, you should see two lines.====此時，你應該能在CDI上看到兩條線。
STRING Once we get on course for the ILS approach, these lines (「needles」) will indicate which direction you need to fly to stay on course.====一旦我們進入ILS進近航路，這些線（「指針」）將指示你保持航道需要的飛行方向。
STRING The vertical needle shows your lateral or horizontal (left/right) deviation from the ILS course. Likewise, the horizontal needle shows your vertical (up/down) deviation.====豎著的指針顯示你的橫向或水平（左/右）ILS航道偏離。同時，橫著的指針顯示你的垂直（上/下）偏離。
STRING If you point the plane』s nose toward the needles (for instance, by flying right when the vertical needle is off to the right, or by flying up when the horizontal needle is up above the horizon line), you』ll eventually intercept the course.====如果你讓機鼻跟隨指針（例如：當垂直指針偏向右邊時向右邊飛，或水平指針高於地平線時向上飛），你最終會截入航道。
STRING Of course, this is all moot for now: we』re perpendicular to the runway, so we won』t start following the ILS guidance until the ATC instructs us to turn toward the runway.====當然，現在這一切都是無意義的：我們現在垂直於跑道，所以直到ATC指示我們轉向跑道前，我們不會開始遵循ILS的引導。
STRING For now, we』ll just continue on heading 070 at 3,000 ft.====現在，我們繼續航向070，高度3,000英尺。
STRING Acknowledge====複誦
STRING Fly heading 160, maintain 5,000 feet... vectors ILS runway 34R at KSEA.====航向160，保持5,000英尺…… 引導到ILS進近KSEA的34R跑道。
STRING Okay, you heard the ATC! Let』s get to a heading of 160 and an altitude of 5,000 ft. We』ll be setting up for an approach to runway 34R.====好的，你聽到ATC說的了！讓我們下到航向160海拔5,000英尺的高度。我們要開始准備34R跑道的進近了。
STRING Use your altimeter and heading indicator to make sure you』re on track.====使用你的高度計和航向指示器，以確保你在航道上。
STRING Remember... we』re aiming for heading 160 and 5,000 ft.====記住，我們的目標是航向160，高度5,000英尺。
STRING That』s great! Hold it right there.====太棒了！把它落在那裏。
STRING We』re currently on downwind for Runway 34R at SeaTac.====我們現在在SeaTac順風的34R跑道上。
STRING You can see the runway to our left...====你可以看到我們左邊的跑道……
STRING Soon, the SeaTac ATC will contact us with the heading and altitude we need to fly on the approach. Until then, we』ll just keep it straight and level.====很快，SeaTac的ATC將會與我們聯系，提供我們所需的航向和高度以及進近程序。在此之前，我們只需要保持水平直線飛行。
STRING Left heading 010, you』re 3 nm from joining, maintain 2,200 ft. until established, clear ILS 34R.====左轉航向010，你從3海裏加入，保持2,200英尺，直到建立盲降，可從34R ILS進近。
STRING Watch your course deviation indicators. When the vertical needle starts moving toward the center, you』ll know you』re almost lined up with the runway, so you need to be moving quickly toward the runway』s heading (340 degrees).====注意你的偏航指示器。當垂直指針開始向中間移動時，你會發現你幾乎與跑道對齊了，現在你需要快速向跑道的方向移動（340度）。
STRING When the CDI is centered, you』ve intercepted the ILS. Just fly in the direction that the needles guide, and you』ll have a perfect approach to the runway.====當CDI居中時，你已經截獲了ILS。只要沿著指針引導的方向飛行，你就可以在跑道上完成一個完美的進近。
STRING Keep in mind that the runway is at heading 340, at an elevation of 433 ft. That will be our heading and altitude by the time we touch down.====請記住，跑道的航向是340，高度是433英尺，當我們著陸時，這也將是我們飛行器的航向與高度。
STRING At this point, when you look at your PFD, you should see two purple diamonds: one on the horizontal axis, one on the vertical axis.====此時此刻，當你看你的PFD時，你應該能看到兩個紫色的菱形：一個在水平軸上，一個在垂直軸上。
STRING Once we get on course for the ILS approach, these diamonds (「needles」) will indicate which direction you need to fly to stay on course.====一旦我們開始了ILS進近，這些菱形（「指針」）將指示你需要飛行的方向，以保持航向。
STRING The vertical needle shows your heading (left/right) deviation from the ILS course. Likewise, the horizontal needle shows your glideslope (up/down) deviation.====垂直指針顯示你的航向（左/右）偏離ILS航道程度。同樣地，水平指針顯示你的下滑道（上/下）偏差。
STRING If you point the plane』s nose toward the needles (for instance, by flying right when vertical needle is off to the right, or by flying up when the horizontal needle is up above the horizon line), you』ll eventually intercept the course.====如果你將機鼻朝向指針（例如：當垂直指針向右移動時向右飛，或者當水平指針向上移動至地平線以上時向上飛），你最終會截獲航道。
STRING Use your primary flight display, or PFD, to monitor your altitude (on the right) and heading (at the bottom).====使用你的主飛行顯示（PFD）來監控你的高度（右側）和航向（底部）。
STRING When you』ve reached 160 degrees, you can tap the HDG button to have the autopilot maintain this heading for you. (It will fly that heading until you tap the button again to turn it off.)====當你轉向160度時，你可以按HDG按鈕，讓自動駕駛儀保持這個航向。（除非你再次按下按鈕關閉它，它會一直維持這個航線）
STRING Just like with your heading, you can tap the ALT button to have the autopilot hold this altitude for you.====就像你的航向一樣，你可以按ALT按鈕讓自動駕駛儀保持這個高度。
STRING Okay, let』s turn left to a heading of 010 degrees and descend to 2,200 ft. We』ll intercept the ILS for runway 34R shortly.====好的，讓我們左轉到010度，下降到2,200英尺，我們很快就會截獲34R跑道的ILS。
STRING Watch your purple course deviation indicators. When the vertical needle starts moving toward the center, you』ll know you』re almost lined up with the runway.====注意你紫色的偏航指示器。當垂直指針開始向中心移動時，你會發現你幾乎和跑道垂直了。
STRING Welcome to X-Plane 11! This is a quick tour to show you around.====歡迎來到X-Plane 11！這個教程會幫助你熟悉熟悉基本操作。
STRING You can dismiss this message by pressing the Enter key, or by clicking 「Continue.」====你可以通過按Enter鍵或單擊「繼續」來忽略此消息。
STRING Let』s talk about how to control the plane.====讓我們來談談如何操控飛機。
STRING You』re using a mouse to fly. Click the mouse near the center of the screen to 「grab」 the yoke (the flight controls). Click a second time if you want to release the controls.====你正在使用鼠標飛行。點擊屏幕中心附近的鼠標來「握住」搖杆（飛機操縱杆）。如果要退出鼠標飛行模式，請再點擊一次。
STRING Practice!====練習！
STRING Move your [control] left or right to roll the plane that direction.====向左或向右移動你的[control]讓飛機傾斜
STRING Move the [control] to the left to make the plane go left!====向左移動[control]讓飛機向左傾斜
STRING Move the [control] to the right to make the plane go right!====向右移動[control]讓飛機向右傾斜
STRING Good work! Keep practicing your turns as long as you』d like.====不錯！現在你可繼續移動以練習你的轉向
STRING Now let』s practice using the [control] to control the airplane』s pitch.====現在我們練習使用[control]來控制飛機的俯仰
STRING Pull the [control] back toward you to raise the nose.====往回拉[control]以使機頭朝上
STRING Push the [control] away from you to lower the nose.====往下推[control]以使機頭朝下
STRING Move the mouse pointer towards the bottom of the box to raise the nose.====將你的鼠標向下移動來抬起機頭
STRING Move the pointer towards the top of the box to lower the nose.====將你的鼠標向上移動來壓低機頭
STRING Well done! Practice bringing the nose up and down until you』re ready to continue.====幹得漂亮！在你准備好下一步之前繼續練習俯仰
STRING I』ll fly the plane for a moment while we learn a few other controls.====在我們學習其他操控動作時我會控制飛機
STRING The throttle controls your engine power, just like the gas pedal in a car. The slider on your joystick is the throttle. Or…====節流閥控制引擎的動力，就像汽車上的油門一樣。操縱杆上的滑塊可以當做節流閥，或者...
STRING The throttle controls your engine power, just like the gas pedal in a car.====節流閥控制引擎的動力，就像汽車上的油門一樣
STRING Push the black knob in the cockpit in to increase the throttle, or pull it out to decrease throttle.====推動駕駛艙內的黑色推杆以增加動力，拉回推杆以減少動力
STRING Increase the throttle all the way to go to full power.====推滿節流閥你將獲得最大動力
STRING This is your airspeed indicator. You can see your speed rising since you added power. Decrease the throttle all the way down to idle and watch the plane slow down again.====這是你的空速指示器，當你增加動力的時候，你可以看見速度正在上升。當你將節流閥減速到慢車時，可以看到飛機又慢了下來。
STRING You can use the keyboard to control the throttle. The 『[throttle_up]』 key increases the throttle.====你可以使用鍵盤來控制節流閥。'[throttle_up]'鍵用於向前推進節流閥
STRING While the 『[throttle_down]』 key decreases it.===='[throttle_down]'鍵用於向後拉回節流閥
STRING Good! I』ll set the throttle to 50% to keep the plane moving nicely.====很好！我會將節流閥設置在50%動力的位置以保持飛機平穩
STRING Commands on the keyboard can change your view. Try pressing 『[view_circle]』 to go to the Circle view.====鍵盤上的按鍵可以改變你的視角。嘗試按下'[view_circle]'來獲得環繞視野
STRING The arrow keys allow you to move the view around.====使用方向鍵可以讓你的視角移動
STRING You can also use the 『[backwards]』 and 『[forwards]』 keys to move your view farther from or closer to the plane.====你也可以使用'[backwards]'和'[forwards]'鍵來讓你的視角遠離或靠近飛機
STRING Let』s go back to the cockpit. Press 『[view_3d_cockpit]』.====讓我們回到駕駛艙，按下'[view_3d_cockpit]'鍵
STRING Zooming can be especially useful in the cockpit to get a good look at your instruments.====縮放能夠使你看清駕駛艙裏的各種儀表狀態
STRING Use the scroll wheel on your mouse to zoom, or the 『[forwards]』 key to get a closer look.====使用鼠標滑輪進行縮放，或使用'[forwards]'鍵以更近觀察
STRING You can bring up the main menu by pressing [sim/operation/show_menu] or by moving your mouse to the top of the screen.====你可以通過按下[sim/operation/show_menu]按鈕或將你的鼠標移到屏幕頂部來喚出主菜單
STRING Options in the menu can change your view. Open the menu by pressing [sim/operation/show_menu] or by moving your mouse to the top of the screen.====菜單裏的選項可以改變你的視角，通過按下[sim/operation/show_menu]按鈕或將你的鼠標移到屏幕頂部來喚出主菜單
STRING Select the Circle view under the View > Change (External) menu.====在視角 > 更改 (外部) 菜單下選擇環繞視角
STRING You can also use the scroll wheel on your mouse to move your view farther from or closer to the plane.====你也可以使用鼠標滑輪來讓你的視角遠離或靠近飛機
STRING Let』s go back to the cockpit view. Open the menu and select the 3-D Panel view, under View > Change (Internal).====讓我們回到駕駛艙視角，打開視角 > 更改 (內部) 菜單，選中 3—D 面板視角
STRING Use the scroll wheel on your mouse to zoom in and out.====使用鼠標滑輪進行縮放
STRING You can pause the simulator at any time by pressing 『[pause]』.====任何時候你都可以通過按下'[pause]'鍵來暫停模擬
STRING Finally, if you need help, just click on the question mark on the right side of the menu bar.====最後，如果你需要幫助，只需點擊菜單欄右側的問號
STRING That』s all you need to know to get started. Why not visit Flight School to check out some more tutorials or customize your own flight in Flight Configuration?====以上就是你在開始模擬前需要知道的內容，為什麼不進入飛行學校去看看更多教程和定制你自己的飛行配置呢？
STRING Remember to extend flaps (『[flaps_down]』). This will make the plane easier to control at low speeds.====記住伸出襟翼 ('[flaps_down]')，這可以讓你在低速時更容易控制飛機
STRING Don』t forget to extend flaps. This will make the plane easier to control at low speeds.====不要忘記放出襟翼，這可以讓你在低速時更容易控制飛機。
STRING Remember you want to gently descend by lowering the throttle.====記住，你要讓飛機慢慢地下降
STRING Your speed is a bit high—raise your nose to slow down a bit.====你的速度有點快——抬高機頭來讓飛機慢一點
STRING Let』s walk through your first takeoff in the Cessna 172SP.====讓我們在賽斯納172SP飛機裏完成你的第一次起飛吧
STRING In a moment I』ll ask you to disengage the parking brake and add full power for takeoff.====不久我會讓你松開停機刹車，推滿推力起飛
STRING Since the C172 is a single-engine propeller aircraft, you will feel the aircraft veer to the left when you』re at high power settings.====C172是一架單引擎螺旋槳飛機，滿推力設定時，你會感受到飛機稍向左偏
STRING Use right rudder to keep the plane in the center of the runway, either by twisting your joystick or using your rudder pedals, if you have them.====如果你擁有方向舵踏板，你可以使用它以向右偏轉方向舵來保持飛機位於跑道中部位置
STRING Use right rudder to keep the plane in the center of the runway by moving your mouse slightly to the right.====向右輕移鼠標以向右偏轉方向舵來保持飛機位於跑道中部位置
STRING Once we reach 55kts, you』ll gently raise the nose of the plane to get off the ground.====當我們到達55節的時候，你可以緩慢抬起機頭來讓飛機離地
STRING Let』s get started!====讓我們開始吧！
STRING Press the 『[brakes]』 key to disengage your parking brakes.====按下'[brakes]'鍵松開停機刹車
STRING First, disengage the brakes.====首先，松開停機刹車
STRING Okay, whenever you』re ready, add full power!====好的，准備好之後隨時可以加滿推力！
STRING (You can press and hold 『[throttle_up]』 to add full power.)====(你可以按住'[throttle_up]'來加滿動力)
STRING (You can push the black knob in all the way to add full power.)====(你可以向前推滿黑色推杆來加滿動力)
STRING Make sure you』re using full power!====確認你使用了滿推力！
STRING Here we go! Watch for 55kts...====來吧，等到55節...
STRING There』s 55 knots! Slowly bring the nose up!====55節！慢慢地抬起機頭
STRING Maintain 74 knots while climbing. If you get too fast, bring the plane』s nose up. If you get too slow, lower the nose.====爬升時保持在74節。如果太快就抬點機頭，如果太慢就壓點機頭
STRING Raise the nose a bit to maintain 74kts during our climb to 1500 feet.====在爬升至1500英尺的過程中，稍微抬高機頭以保持74節空速
STRING Raise the nose slightly, so that your speed slowly goes back down to 74kts during the climb.====輕抬機頭，這樣在爬升時你的空速可以回到74節
STRING Lower the nose a bit to maintain 74kts during our climb to 1500 feet.====在爬升至1500英尺的過程中，稍微壓低機頭以保持74節空速
STRING Raise the nose to climb to 1500 feet.====抬高機頭爬升至1500英尺
STRING This is your altimeter. Read it like a clock. The small hand is thousands of feet. The big hand is hundreds of feet.====這是你的高度計。看高度表就像看鍾，小圈指針每個數字代表一千英尺，大圈指針每個數字代表一百英尺。
STRING Continue climbing until you reach 1500 ft.====繼續爬升至1500英尺
STRING There』s 750 ft! You』re halfway to 1500, so keep climbing!====這裏是750英尺，上到1500英尺的進度已經過半了，繼續爬升吧
STRING At 1400 feet, slowly start lowering the nose to level off right at 1500 feet.====在1400英尺，需緩慢壓低機頭以正好到達1500英尺
STRING This is your vertical speed indicator, or 「VSI.」 The needle points up when you』re climbing and down when you』re descending.====這是你的垂直速度指示器，在你爬升時指針朝上，在下降時指針朝下。
STRING Since you want to level off here at 1500 ft, you want to try to keep the VSI needle at 0.====如果你想要正好到達1500英尺，你需要試著讓垂直速度指示器的指針指向0
STRING Climb back up to 1,500 feet.====爬升至1500英尺
STRING Descend back down to 1,500 feet.====下降至1500英尺
STRING Level off to maintain 1,500 feet.====拉平機頭以保持在1500英尺
STRING Great! Hold the plane level right here!====很好！保持在這個高度
STRING We』re a bit high. Let』s descend back down to 1100 ft.====我們有點高了，下降到1100英尺
STRING Now that we』re in the crosswind phase of the pattern, you can go ahead and lower the throttle to about 70% to cruise.====現在我們進入已經進入側風邊（「第三邊」），你可以繼續向前，回拉節流閥至70%處以保持巡航
STRING Looking good! We』ve entered the upwind phase of the traffic pattern. Let』s aim to maintain about 1100 ft as we circle around.====看起來不錯！我們已經進入進場航線的離場邊（「第二邊」）。我們繞跑道一圈時請保持高度在1100英尺。
STRING We』re ready to fly our first traffic pattern!====我們已經准備好進行我們的第一次五邊飛行了！
STRING We』re just going to take off, circle around parallel to the runway, then turn back toward the runway to land right back here.====我們剛剛起飛，盤旋使飛機與跑道平行，然後回轉對准跑道並降落
STRING Follow the green checkpoint markers for a perfect pattern.====通過綠色的檢查點，以進行一次完美的五邊。
STRING We』ve entered the downwind phase of the pattern. I』m going to take the controls for a moment...====我們現在處於路線的順風邊，我一會兒准備控制飛機
STRING You can keep yourself oriented during the pattern by looking over your shoulder at the runway.====你可以觀察自己肩膀後方相對跑道的位置以確認並保持自己的方位
STRING Remember that you can re-center your view by pressing 『[view_3d_cockpit]』.====你可以通過按下'[view_3d_cockpit]'鍵來使視角回中

STRING It』s incredibly difficult to control a helicopter with only the mouse. It』s probably a good idea to return to Flight School and try something different for now.====只使用鼠標控制直升機是非常困難的，也許您可以回到飛行學校嘗試一些不同的東西

STRING Welcome to your first helicopter flight. We』ll start off learning to hover.====歡迎來到你的第一次直升機飛行訓練，我們從懸停開始學習。
STRING The collective controls how much lift your main rotor generates, which in turns controls your upward motion.====總矩控制你的主旋翼產生多少升力，為飛機提供向上的動力。
STRING The more collective you add, the more lift you』ll generate.====總矩越多，升力越大
STRING So, to hover just above the ground, you』ll only need a little collective—maybe 30%.====所以只是盤旋在低空的話，你只需要小動力的總矩—大約30%
STRING You can use the throttle on your joystick to control the collective. Or press 『[sim/engines/prop_up]』 to increase it or 『[sim/engines/prop_down]』 to decrease it.====你可以使用遙杆上的節流閥來控制總矩，或按下'[sim/engines/prop_up]'來增加總距，按下'[sim/engines/prop_up]'來減少總矩
STRING The throttle lever on your joystick controls the collective.====遙杆上的節流閥操縱杆可以控制總矩
STRING As you』re using the collective to lift off the ground, you』ll need to move your [control] forward or back to keep from drifting.====當你增加總矩離地的時候，你需要向前或向後移動你的[control]來防止飛機晃動
STRING If you drift forward, tilt your [control] back to stay in place.====如果你向前傾斜，往回拉[control]以保持平衡
STRING Likewise, if you drift back, tilt your [control] forward a bit.====同樣的，如果你向後傾斜，那就向前推一點[control]
STRING Be careful, though! It』s easy to over-control and go too far. It takes only the tiniest movements of the controls to stay in place.====一定要小心！這很容易過度操控而飛遠，你只需要稍微動一動操控就足夠保持位置不變。
STRING Finally, your anti-torque pedals control your tail rotor, which in turn controls how much you rotate left & right.====最後，你的反扭矩踏板控制你的尾旋翼，這個控制你向左或向右轉向的角度。
STRING As you hover, you』ll need to keep the pedals just a tad to the left (and hold them there) to keep the helicopter pointed straight down the runway.====當你盤旋的時候，你需要稍微向左或保持住踏板來保證直升機正對跑道。

STRING At low speeds in a taildragger, you』ll need to pull back on the [control] slightly to keep the nose up and the tail wheel firmly on the ground. Otherwise, you』ll lose the ability to steer!====後三點式飛機在低速時你需要稍微向後拉[control]一點來保持機鼻朝上並且尾輪觸地。不然的話你就沒法轉向了！

STRING Note that as you get closer to the VOR, the radials will get closer together, so smaller changes to your course will produce bigger changes on the course deviation indicator.====注意到當你接近甚高頻全向信標時，指針會越來越近，所以對你飛行路線的小改動會造成儀表上大的變動。
STRING We』re ready to start navigating to Juneau International. I』m going to fly for a moment to get you oriented.====我們准備好導航到朱諾國際機場了。我將會飛一段時間，幫你把一把方位。
STRING We』re flying the 295 radial to the Sisters Island VOR. The VOR transmitter is like the hub of a bike wheel, and it sends out 360 radials—the 「spokes」 of the wheel—to tell you where you are in relation to the 「hub.」====我們在朝著295信號源去到Sisters Island的甚高頻全向信標（VOR）。VOR就像一個車輪的輪軸一樣，向外面360度廣播-或者說像是車輪的「輻條」一樣-告訴你和「輪軸」的相對位置。
STRING So, we』re going to follow one of these 「spokes」 (radials) to reach Sisters Island, and then we』ll follow another radial away from Sisters Island to get to Juneau.====所以我們要跟著其中的一個「輻條」去到Sisters Island，然後我們會跟著另一個信號源從Sisters Island到朱諾。
STRING Now, we』re on the 295 radial, but since the radials are measured as the heading when going away from the VOR, and we』re instead going toward it, that means we'll fly a course of 115 degrees (the inverse heading of 295).====現在，我們在295航向上。但是現在這個295指針表示的是離信標越來越遠的航向（「背台」），但是我們是向著信標飛行（「向台」），所以我們需要調整我們的飛行航路到115度（295度的相反方向）。
STRING Take a look at your course deviation indicator, or CDI.====看一下你的偏航指示器（CDI）。
STRING The vertical bar here is the lateral (horizontal) course deviation indicator. The CDI shows where our course is in relation to the aircraft itself.====豎條是水平偏航指示。CDI顯示的是飛機（位於儀表正中央）與航路（儀表的豎線）的相對位置。
STRING Since I』ve tuned our navigation radio to fly the 295 radial of the Sisters Island VOR, and we』re right on track for that radial, you can see that the CDI is centered.====因為我校准了我們的導航到Sisters Island VOR的295指針，我們又正好在航線上，所以你可以看到CDI指針在正中的位置。
STRING But, watch what happens when we drift off course.====但是，注意當我們偏離航線時會發生什麼。
STRING Do you see the vertical course deviation indicator drifting to the left of center? It indicates that, since we』ve deviated to the right, we need to adjust our course to the left to re-intercept the radial.====你注意到儀表上的豎線往左邊偏移了嗎？這代表我們正在向右偏，我們需要向左調整我們的航線來重新攔截指針。
STRING If you look out the window, you』ll see that the 295 radial is over to our left—this agrees with the vertical course deviation indicator.====如果你往窗外看，你將會看見295指針在我們的左邊-這與我們的偏航儀顯示的方位保持一致。
STRING Let』s get back on track.====讓我們回到航線上。
STRING The key here is not to over-correct. We want to turn just a bit toward the direction the CDI indicates, then wait.====這裏重要的是不要過度糾正。我們只要向CDI指示的方向轉一點然後只要等著就好了。
STRING If, after a few seconds, we don』t see the CDI bar moving, we』ll deviate a bit farther toward the left.====如果幾秒鍾後我們並沒有發現CDI豎線移動，我們可以向左再轉一點。
STRING As you can see, the vertical bar is starting to come back toward the center, so we need to turn back to be lined up with the radial.====你可以看見，豎線現在開始向儀表中心回攏，所以我們需要轉回去來對准指針。
STRING Okay, at this point, you know all you need to fly the VOR. So, we』re going to head to Sisters Island (the site of the VOR we』re getting guidance from) and from there go on to Juneau International.====好了，在這個時間點上你已經知道了所有你該知道的用VOR飛行的東西。所以，我們將飛往Sisters Island（VOR的地點）然後從那裏飛往朱諾國際機場。
STRING Just follow the guidance from the course deviation indicator and we』ll reach Sisters Island in no time.====只要跟著偏航儀走我們一會就能到Sisters Island了。
STRING Okay, we』re over the Sisters Island VOR... Remember, this is like being at the hub of a bike wheel.====好了，我們到達了Sisters Island的VOR了......記住，這就像是在自行車輪子正中央的輪軸上一樣。
STRING We』re now going to fly the 035 radial out of the hub. Start flying away from the hub for a bit, and watch your CDI closely.====現在我們將從035指針飛出這裏。開始向外飛行一點，然後仔細看著你的CDI。
STRING When the needle starts to move, turn to heading 035, then begin correcting your heading to center the CDI again.====當指針開始移動，轉向航向035時再開始把航線往CDI中間調整。
STRING You can picture the VOR radial like the series of hoops you see in the sky. The hoops start at the VOR transmitter and continue for many miles in a straight line.====你可以把VOR想象成在天上的指針。指針從VOR發射器開始一條直線綿延很多英裏。
STRING The VOR transmitter creates 360 lines like this—one line for each compass degree around the transmitter.====VOR發射器向四周發射出總共360條像這樣的線，每一度一條線。
STRING We』re on the 295 radial—the line coming from the VOR transmitter at heading 295. The hoops in front of us visualize that radial.====我們現在在295指針上-從VOR天線以295航向發過來的。我們前面的線代表著那條線。
STRING Take a look at your primary flight display.====看一下你的飛行主控顯示器。
STRING The purple diamond here (beneath the artificial horizon) is the course deviation indicator, or CDI. The CDI shows where our course is in relation to the aircraft itself.====這個紫色鑽石型的東西（在人工地平儀下面）是偏航儀或CDI。CDI顯示我們航線與飛機相對的位置。
STRING Since I』ve tuned our navigation radio to fly the 295 radial of the Sisters Island VOR, and we』re right on track for that radial, the you can see that the CDI is centered.====因為我校准了我們的導航到Sisters IslandVOR的295指針，我們正好在航線上，你可以看到CDI在正中的位置。
STRING Do you see the purple course deviation indicator drifting to the left of center? It indicates that, since we』ve deviated to the right, we need to adjust our course to the left to re-intercept the radial.====你注意到紫色的偏航顯示往左邊偏移了嗎？這代表我們正在向右偏，我們需要向左調整我們的航線來重新攔截指針。
STRING If you look out the window, you』ll see that the 295 radial is over to our left—this agrees with the purple course deviation indicator.====如果你往窗外看，你將會看見295指針在我們的左邊-這與我們的紫色偏航顯示保持一致。
STRING If, after a few seconds, we don』t see the CDI diamond moving, we』ll deviate a bit farther toward the left.====如果幾秒鍾後我們並沒有發現紫色鑽石型標志移動，我們會向左再轉一點。
STRING As you can see, the diamond is starting to come back toward the center, so we need to turn back to be lined up with the radial.====你可以看見，紫色的鑽石形標志現在開始向儀表中心回攏，所以我們需要轉回去來對准指針。
